We all need to Start the registration fee of (rs: 10000/- or 5000/- depending on the work) for those clients who wants us to do the ground work/home work on their requirement. Benefits of Charging the regn fee/advance fee

1. With regn fee Clients will aproach us only if they are serious.

2. Once they pay the regn fee client will be with us and he will not aproach other brokers .
So we can  work with other realtor and close it. 
3. With regn fee our effort of attending the clients and doing the visits will not get wasted. 

4. If the client did not close the deal then Atleast All our expences of the visut will be covered including the time.

5. We will save lot of time and energy which we can use for genuine clients or to some other personal works.

6.the more we get regn fee then more we get fund. 

7. Time passers will stay away.

8. We will be getting paid for the consultation. 

Kindly share your comments. 
With all your support and unity we can create a new bench mark in real esttae.
